<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a> (2255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrómnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скромне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скромне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>modest, humble</li>
<li>modest, frugal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заработок.html>за́работок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrómnyj</b> zárabotok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">modest earnings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrómnyj</b> obéd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frugal dinner</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>modest, unassuming, unpretentious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наряд.html>наря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrómnyj</b> narjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">modest/simple attire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>слу́жащий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrómnyj</b> slúžaščij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lowly clerk</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мному</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po mojemú <b>skrómnomu</b> mnéniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in my humble opinion</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>modest, prudish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrómnyj</b> výrez na plátʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a modest neckline on a dress</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скромный.html>скро́мный</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slíškom <b>skrómnyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">overmodest; overly modest</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***скрупулезно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрупулезно.html>скрупулёзно</a> (25432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрупулезно.html>скрупулёзно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrupuljózno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрупулезно.html>скрупулёзно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrupuljózno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>скру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лёз<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-скрупулёзн-</b>; суффикс: <b>-о</b>.

***скрутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a> (8182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to roll</li>
<li>to bind, to tie up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrutítʹ</b> rúki komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pinion someone's arms; pinion someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring into submission, to subdue, to overmaster
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бараний.html>бара́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skrutítʹ v baránij rog</i> ― <span class="e-translation">make knuckle under; make toe the line</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(disease)</i> to overpower, to attack, to seize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:паралич.html>парали́ч</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>skrutíl</b> paralíč</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was paralyzed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá <b>skrutílo</b> ot bóli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I had an attack/paroxysm of rending pain</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивать</a> (22333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to roll</li>
<li>to bind, to tie up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrúčivatʹ</b> rúki komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pinion someone's arms; pinion someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring into submission, to subdue, to overmaster</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(disease)</i> to overpower, to attack, to seize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрывать.html>скрыва́ть</a> (1881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрывать.html>скрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hide, to conceal</li>
<li>to dissemble, to keep back</li>
<li>to keep secret</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скры́тие</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skrýtije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрытный.html>скры́тный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skrýtnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрывать.html>скрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрываться.html>скрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыться.html>скры́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappear; to hide from; to go into hiding</li>
<li>to escape; to steal away; to sneak away; to slip away</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрывать.html>скрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрывший.html>скры́вший</a> (3636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a> (3636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрывать.html>скрыва́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрыться.html>скры́ться</a> (2007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыться.html>скры́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрываться.html>скрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappear, to hide from, to go into hiding</li>
<li>to escape, to steal away</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрыть.html>скрыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:невидимый.html>неви́димым</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:недоступный.html>недосту́пным</a></i>.
</p>

***скудный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a> (8520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Constructed as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скуда́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skudá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poverty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">скудъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skudŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">скѫдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skǫdŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skǫd-</i>; see also pre-first-palatalization <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skęd-</i>, whence <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щадить.html>щади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščadítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spare, to have mercy on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬯𐬗𐬀𐬥𐬛𐬀𐬌𐬌𐬈𐬌𐬥𐬙𐬌</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">scandaiieinti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">they destroy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬯𐬐𐬆𐬥𐬛𐬀</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skənda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">broken; illness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scandula</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shingles</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scindula</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skúdnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скудне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скудне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scant, scanty, meagre <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, in something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnyje</b> zapásy vodý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scant water supply</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доход.html>дохо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnyj</b> doxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slender/meagre income</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>сведе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnyje</b> svedénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scant information; scanty reports</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словарный.html>слова́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnyj</b> slovárnyj zapás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scant vocabulary</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnyj</b> um</i> ― <span class="e-translation">feeble mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>poor, pathetic, wretched</li>
<li>poor, infertile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skúdnaja</b> póčva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">poor soil</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скука.html>ску́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скука.html>ску́ки</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

***скула.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>скула́</a> (6544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>скула́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skulá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>скулы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>ску́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>ску́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheekbone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a curved corner of a ship's hull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">between bow and sides, or between stern and sides</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; a bilge between the bottom and side plating</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a side of a ship’s bow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">«тита́ник» <a href = vnd.unilang:налететь.html>налете́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:айсберг.html>а́йсберг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>скуло́й</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">“Titánik” naletél na ájsberg právoj <b>skulój</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Titanic hit the iceberg with her starboard bow.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скуластый.html>скула́стый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skulástyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скуловой</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skulovoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">высокоскулый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vysokoskulyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">узкоскулый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uzkoskulyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скуластый.html>скула́стый</a> (15393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***скульптура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́ра</a> (6507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skulʹptúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the singular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sculpture (art of sculpting)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the singular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sculpture (collective, the works of a sculptor)</li>
<li>sculpture (a sculpted piece)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***скупать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скупать.html>скупа́ть</a> (17355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скупить.html>скупи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to buy up, to corner (e.g. shares)</li></ol>
